<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:foppen.html>foppen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to trick</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:speen.html>speen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">teat, nipple</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fopspeen.html>fopspeen</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fopspeen.html>fopspenen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fopspeen.html>fopspeentje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <span class="Latn" lang="en">dummy</span>, a <span class="Latn" lang="en">pacifier</span>, a comforter. <span class="defdate">[from 1890s]</span>

</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:forceps.html>forceps</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:forceps.html>forceps</a></strong></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">forcipes</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">forcepses</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>An instrument used in surgery or medical <a href = vnd.unilang:procedures.html>procedures</a> for grasping and holding <a href = vnd.unilang:objects.html>objects</a>, similar to <a href = vnd.unilang:tongs.html>tongs</a> or pincers.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Although the Latin word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> singular, this word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> often treated as a plurale tantum by analogy with names for similar <a href = vnd.unilang:items.html>items</a> such as <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tongs.html>tongs</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tweezers</i>: <i>this <a href = vnd.unilang:forceps.html>forceps</a></i> or <i>these <a href = vnd.unilang:forceps.html>forceps</a></i> (or <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> <i>pair of <a href = vnd.unilang:forceps.html>forceps</a></i>).
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">pair of <a href = vnd.unilang:forceps.html>forceps</a></span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">microforceps</span></li></ul>

</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:tang.html>tang</a></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:forel.html>forel</a> (15431)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Forelle</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">forhel</i>, older <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">forhen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">forhana</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:forel.html>forel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:forellen.html>forellen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:forel.html>forelletje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A trout, <i>Salmo trutta</i>.</li>
<li>One of certain fish of the subfamily Salmoninae, specifically certain members of the genera <i>Salvelinus</i> and <i>Oncorhynchus</i>.</li></ol>

***foreman.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:foreman.html>foreman</a> (10924)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">fore-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">foarman</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:voorman.html>voorman</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Vormann</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">formand</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">förman</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">formaður</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:foreman.html>foreman</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">foremen</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">management</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The leader of a work crew.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">law</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The member of a <a href = vnd.unilang:jury.html>jury</a> who presides <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> it and speaks on its behalf.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> during the era of slavery</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A black (slave) assistant to the white overseer who managed field hands.</li></ol>

<p>Probably borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:forens.html>Forens</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">forēnsis</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">of or pertaining to the market</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***forensisch.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:forensisch.html>forensisch</a> (8937)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:forensisch.html>forensisch</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">forensis</i>, from forum (public square where Roman public legal proceedings <a href = vnd.unilang:took.html>took</a> place)
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:forensisch.html>forensisch</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>legal, court <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a>, trial <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a></li>
<li>especially, forensic, relating to the use of science and technology in the investigation and establishment of <a href = vnd.unilang:facts.html>facts</a> or evidence in a court of law</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gerechtelijk.html>gerechtelijk</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gerecht.html>gerecht</a></span>s-, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wet.html>wet</a></span>s-</li></ul>
<hr />
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijvoeglijk_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijvoeglijk.html>Bijvoeglijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:forensisch.html>forensisch</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:juridisch.html>juridisch</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:betrekking.html>betrekking</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hebbend.html>hebbend</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:justitie.html>justitie</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:specialiseerde.html>specialiseerde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> in <b><a href = vnd.unilang:forensische.html>forensische</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:geneeskunde.html>geneeskunde</a>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:forgotten.html>forgotten</a> (131040)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:forgotten.html>forgotten</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">more <a href = vnd.unilang:forgotten.html>forgotten</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">most <a href = vnd.unilang:forgotten.html>forgotten</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Of which knowledge <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lost.html>lost</a>; which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> no longer remembered.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:forgotten.html>forgotten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">forget</i></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:forgotten.html>forgotten</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">forgottens</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A person or thing that <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:forgotten.html>forgotten</a>.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2007</b> December 31,  Alan Feuer,  “Headliners of 07: A Subway Savior, Rampaging <a href = vnd.unilang:rats.html>Rats</a>, and a $12 Million Dog”, in  <cite>New York Times</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2007/12/31/nyregion/31onehits.html">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Luckily for these unfortunate <b>forgottens</b>, New Year <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> approaching, a time when, despite the intuitions of the calendar, our thoughts often turn to the past.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>

***formaldehyde.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:formaldehyde.html>formaldehyde</a> (27674)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:formaldehyde.html>formaldehyde</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">formaldehydes</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">organic chemistry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The simplest aldehyde, H-CHO, a colourless gas that <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> many industrial applications; it dissolves in water to give formol (10%) and formalin.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">H-CHO</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">E240</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">when used as a preservative</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, methanal <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">IUPAC name</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ul>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:formuleren.html>formuleren</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to word</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i>.

***formulier.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:formulier.html>formulier</a> (6367)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">formulaire</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">formularium</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">form (collection)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, itself from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">formula</i> (diminutive of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:forma.html>forma</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">form, shape</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>) + <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">-arium</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-ary</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The current sense <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Formular</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:formulier.html>formulier</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:formulieren.html>formulieren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:formulier.html>formuliertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A form, a formally standardized (often printed) document to fill out in order to file a specific request, declaration etc.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">forneise</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">fornoise</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">fornaise</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">fornāx</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fornuis.html>fornuis</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fornuizen.html>fornuizen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fornuis.html>fornuisje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>cooker, <a href = vnd.unilang:stuiven.html>stove</a> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">kitchen appliance consisting of a cooktop and an <a href = vnd.unilang:oven.html>oven</a></span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***fossiel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:fossiel.html>fossiel</a> (18632)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">fossile</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">fossilis</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">something which <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> dug up</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">fodio</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I dig up</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. First attested in the early 19th century.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fossiel.html>fossiel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fossielen.html>fossielen</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">fossiliën</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fossiel.html>fossieltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">fossil</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> someone with very old fashioned ideas, a dinosaur</li></ol>

***fotografie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:fotografie.html>fotografie</a> (14362)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">foto-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-grafie</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fotografie.html>fotografie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fotografie.html>fotografieën</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">fotografies</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fotografie.html>fotografietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:fraai.html>fraai</a> (6598)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vrai</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">verai</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">vērāx</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">truthful</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<ol><li>beautiful, pretty, handsome</li>
<li>nice, fancy</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">fraction</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">frāctiō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a fragment, portion</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***fractuur.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:fractuur.html>fractuur</a> (65135)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">fracture</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">fracture</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">fractura</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a breach, fracture, cleft</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">frangere</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to break</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, past participle <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">fractus</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bʰreg-</i>, from whence also English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">break</i> and Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:breken.html>breken</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***franc.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:franc.html>franc</a> (11961)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:franc.html>franc</a></i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid aaa; font-size: 90%; background: f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English Wikipedia <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/franc" class="extiw" title="w:franc"><a href = vnd.unilang:franc.html>franc</a></a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/franc" class="extiw" title="w:franc">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:franc.html>franc</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:francs.html>francs</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A former unit of currency of France, Belgium and Luxembourg, replaced by the euro.</li>
<li>Any of several units of currency, some of which are multi-national (West African CFA <a href = vnd.unilang:franc.html>Franc</a> (XOF), Central African CFA <a href = vnd.unilang:franc.html>Franc</a> (XAF), the Swiss <a href = vnd.unilang:franc.html>franc</a> (CHF)) while others are national currencies.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The word <a href = vnd.unilang:franc.html>franc</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> abbreviated 'F' in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ISO_4217" class="extiw" title="w:ISO 4217">ISO 4217</a> currency <a href = vnd.unilang:codes.html>codes</a>, usually prepended by the country's 2-letter alpha code in the case of national currencies:
</p>
<ul><li>BIF: Burundi <a href = vnd.unilang:franc.html>Franc</a></li>
<li>CDF: Congolese <a href = vnd.unilang:franc.html>Franc</a></li>
<li>CHF: Swiss <a href = vnd.unilang:franc.html>franc</a></li>
<li>DJF: Djibouti <a href = vnd.unilang:franc.html>Franc</a></li>
<li>GNF: Guinean <a href = vnd.unilang:franc.html>Franc</a></li>
<li>KMF: Comorian <a href = vnd.unilang:franc.html>Franc</a></li>
<li>RAF: Rwandan <a href = vnd.unilang:franc.html>Franc</a></li>
